<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учительский.html>учи́тельское</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жалование.html>жалова́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učítelʹskoje</b> žalovánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">teacher's salary</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***учить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a> (1285)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">учити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*učiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выучить.html>вы́учить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:научить.html>научи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обучить.html>обучи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to teach, to instruct
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:научить.html>научи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обучить.html>обучи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to learn; to study</li>
<li>to memorize by rote</li>
<li>to punish, to beat, to whip</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>чи́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:выучить.html>вы́учить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:научить.html>научи́ть</a>.

***учиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a> (907)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">учити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*učiti</i> and <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sę</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">učítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выучиться.html>вы́учиться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:научиться.html>научи́ться</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> reflexive<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> passive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> - reflexive and passive verb for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">reflexive for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to learn, to study
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>у́чится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йскому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языку́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>účitsja</b> anglíjskomu jazykú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he’s learning English</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собственный.html>со́бственных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бках</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učítʹsja</b> na sóbstvennyx ošíbkax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn from one’s mistakes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>век</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живи́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>век</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́сь</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vek živí, vek <b>učísʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">live and learn</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">live a century, learn a century</span>”)</div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>век</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живи́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>век</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́сь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дурако́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помереть.html>помрёшь</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sarcastic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vek živí, vek <b>učísʹ</b>, a durakóm pomrjóšʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the more you know, the more you forget</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">live a century, learn a century, and you’ll die a fool</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздно.html>по́здно</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učítʹsja</b> nikogdá ne pózdno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is never too late to learn</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>уму́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупость.html>глу́пости</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мудрость.html>му́дрости</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чужой.html>чужи́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бках</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverbs</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>učísʹ</b> umú na čužój glúposti; <b>učísʹ</b> múdrosti na čužíx ošíbkax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">learn wisdom by the follies of others</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">reflexive for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to study (at), to learn (from somebody), to be an apprentice (to somebody)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>у́чится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:университет.html>университе́те</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>účitsja</b> v universitéte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he studies at the university</span></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">passive for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учить.html>учи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">učítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to be taught

(2)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">któ-l. (1) <b>účitsja</b> u kovó-l. (2)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">somebody (1) is taught by somebody (2)</span></div>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>


<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>чи́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <span>приставочные <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:выучиться.html>вы́учиться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:научиться.html>научи́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-уч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ша́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тый</b>

Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>уша́стее, уша́стей, поуша́стее, поуша́стей.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-уш-</b>; суффикс: <b>-аст</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ши́б</b>

***ущемить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a> (23716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щемить.html>щеми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščemítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščemítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемлять.html>ущемля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pinch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">morally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to infringe, to restrict, to restrain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a></b> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uščemítʹ</b> čʹí-libo pravá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>infringe</b> upon someone's rights</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to offend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uščemítʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>offend</b> someone's self-esteem</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uščemítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемление.html>ущемле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščemlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемление.html>ущемле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемление.html>ущемле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемление.html>ущемле́ний</a></b>)

<ol><li>pinching, strangulation</li>
<li>infringement, encroachment (e.g. on rights)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uščemítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемлять.html>ущемля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščemljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемить.html>ущеми́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pinch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">morally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to infringe, to restrict, to restrain

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to offend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ущемлять.html>ущемля́ть</a></b> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uščemljátʹ</b> čʹjó-libo samoljúbije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>offend</b> someone's self-esteem</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ущербность.html>уще́рбность</a> (27327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербный.html>уще́рбный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uščérbnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербность.html>уще́рбность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščérbnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербность.html>уще́рбности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербность.html>уще́рбности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербность.html>уще́рбностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>defectiveness, inferiority</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущерб.html>уще́рб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uščérb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербный.html>уще́рбный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščérbnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(moon)</i> on the wane, waning</li>
<li>defective
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ущербный.html>уще́рбная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:психика.html>пси́хика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uščérbnaja</b> psíxika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">defective state of mind; mental degeneration</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ущипнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ущипнуть.html>ущипну́ть</a> (20403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">щипну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščipnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ущипнуть.html>ущипну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uščipnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ущи́пывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pinch <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with fingers or a beak</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
